 It is said that the major component of culture is the slow pace of language and it rarely crosses geographical boundaries
 is vajah se samskruti kaa prasar dhimaa hota he or vah praaia: ek kshetra vishesh tak simit hokar rah jaati he
 But due to the proliferation of technology along with the number and richness of Hindi speakers, this common language of North India is breaking many boundaries

 With the popularity of Internet-based apps and websites, the speed of language spread is no longer slow
